; --- INDEX ---
;
; lines starting with ; as first non-whitespace are comments
;
; File format is single lines formatted as Key:Value
;
; KEYS
; page:comic page ID and link: heads a comic page entry.
; 	auth: Author / artist page comment or note
; 	date: date of the page, preferably YYYY-MM-DD
; 	desc: text relevant to the page (title / description / line of dialogue, etc)
; 	note: footnotes, links, etc
; 	tag: tags for the page's story items of note: character, item, location, etc.
; baseurl: default url applies to any following page:without a url: key
; (to insert pageID replace in baseurl/url with {0} )
;
; Can use multiple tag: per page, but only one of each of the other keys
;
; desc:, note: and auth: text's internal formatting is a mix of [Markdown](http://daringfireball.net/projects/markdown) plus html (for <br> etc)
; **bold**
; _italic_
; [internal link text](#sometag) - tag links are lower case
; [external link text](http://www.gunnerkrigg.com)
; tags starting ch-* are treated separately as chapter identifiers -- not used for Wapsi at present
;
; What's tagged
;
; Who 
;     - known, named characters on-page: Monica, Jin
;     - speaking generics: PoliceMan, Policeman2
;     - significant reference to an off-page character
; Where
;     - general location (Monica's House not Monica's Bedroom)
;     - Dreams - from daydreams to nightmares
; What
;     - props and details _when significant_: typically Phone is tagged when used, not just shown in background as a phone on a desk
;     - symbolism (when blatant enough for yr humble tagger to spot it)
; When
;     - in-comic significant dates, e.g. Halloween
;     - flashbacks to earlier events
; Specific rather than general 
;     - Daren's Bar (specific) is not tagged as a Bar (generic) as well
;     - Phix is tagged with Sphinx on early appearances, but thereafter only if strongly displaying the Sphinx nature
; Meta
;   - _e.g._ fillers, guest comics, art pages, special colour pages (for a b&w comic)
;
baseurl: http://wapsisquare.com/comic/{0}/
; Amanda
; Atsali
; Castela
;
